\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

    \subsection{test the pylamost}\label{test-the-pylamost}

    In order to access protected LAMOST data, you should provide your token.
Your token can be obtained from http://dr.lamost.org/ucenter/mytoken,
the "Password" is the token. When you get your token you can also create
a file \texttt{\textasciitilde{}/pylamost.ini} or
\texttt{\%userprofile\%/pylamost.ini} on Windows, with content:

\begin{verbatim}
token=12345678
\end{verbatim}

Then you don't have to write the token next time.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}1}]:} \PY{k+kn}{from} \PY{n+nn}{pylamost} \PY{k}{import} \PY{n}{lamost}
        \PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{lamost}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}init the lamost class}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}lm.token=\PYZsq{}12345678\PYZsq{}\PYZsh{}specify your token. You can pass this step, if you created the \PYZti{}/pylamost.ini file.}
        \PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dataset}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{5} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}specify the Data Release number}
        \PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{version}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}specify the data version, or leave it None to always use the leatest version.}
\end{Verbatim}


    \subsubsection{Query interface}\label{query-interface}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{n}{params}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{output.fmt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{csv}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{obsidTextarea}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{353301001}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
        \PY{n}{hl}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{query}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{params}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{hl}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

        \PY{n}{files}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{pos.posfile}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sample.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{open}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sample.txt}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
        \PY{n}{hl}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{query2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{params}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{files}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{hl}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsubsection{read local spectrum fits to data
array}\label{read-local-spectrum-fits-to-data-array}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}13}]:} \PY{n}{wavelength}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{specflux}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}7}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}15}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{readFits}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{spec\PYZhy{}57278\PYZhy{}EG224429N215706B01\PYZus{}sp01\PYZhy{}001.fits.gz}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(\PYZsq{}wavelength\PYZsq{}, wavelength)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(\PYZsq{}specflux\PYZsq{}, specflux)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(\PYZsq{}spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}7\PYZsq{}, spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}7)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print(\PYZsq{}spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}15\PYZsq{}, spec\PYZus{}smooth\PYZus{}15)}
\end{Verbatim}
